NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

G. ISHITHA
8th January 2020.
 
A. Prabhu, a male child born to Thiru. S. Arumugam on 9th September 1984, residing at No.2/2.1, Kavalkara Street,
Poigaiputhur, Krishnarayapuram, Karur District-639 102, has been living as female after an elaborate sexual reassignment
surgery by Dr. S. Saravana Kumar, Mahatma Gandhi Medical College & Research Institute, Pillaiyarkuppam, Puducherry
(Reg. No: 76831). By this, I may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as PRAHASINI.A
Chennai, 
A. PRABHU
9th January 2020.
